<h2 class="hwp-hero__title hwp-order-2 h1" id="">
    People
  </h2>
<div class="hwp-hero__description hwp-order-3 hwp-text-block">
<div class="hwp-text-block field field--name-field-hwp-body field--type-text-long field--label-hidden"><p>IQSS is comprised of a community of exceptional scholars and staff, who collaborate on and provide support for a wide range of social science research.</p></div>
</div>

<h2 class="h2 hwp-tabs__panel-title">Visitors &amp; Affiliates</h2>

<article class="page-card page-card--horizontal page-card--hwp-person page-card--teaser page-card-- hwp-bg-light-base" data-component-name="page-card" lang="en">
<div class="page-card__text hwp-order-1">
<a class="page-card__link hwp-order-2" href="/people/dylan-carlson-sirvent-le%C3%B3n"> <h3 class="page-card__heading hwp-order-2">Dylan  Carlson Sirvent León</h3>

<div class="page-card__subheading hwp-order-2">
